Omon: Pangeo CMIP6 Dataset Catalog - historical monthly ocean data¶

Catalog URL:

https://raw.githubusercontent.com/pangeo-data/pangeo-datastore/master/intake-catalogs/cmip6_Omon.yaml

Parent Catalogs¶

master / cmip6

Datasets¶

BCC_CSM2_MR.historical.r1i1p1f1.sos¶

CMIP6 monthly Sea Surface Salinity for BCC-CSM2-MR historical r1i1p1f1

load in python 

import intake
cat = intake.Catalog("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/pangeo-data/pangeo-datastore/master/intake-catalogs/cmip6_Omon.yaml")
ds = cat["BCC_CSM2_MR.historical.r1i1p1f1.sos"].to_dask()

metadata

uploader_githubnaomi-henderson
uploader_emailnhn2@columbia.edu
tags['ocean', 'model']
catalog_dir/home/jovyan/./intake-catalogs/
